'''Claflin doctrine''' is a [[United States law|U.S. law doctrine]] which states that the trust cannot be modified or terminated, even if all beneficiaries agree, if to do so would be contrary to a material purpose of the [[settlor]]. Material purposes include [[Spendthrift trust|spendthrift]], support, and [[discretionary trust]]s.
